Source Code

This is the source-code for the Apollo 9 Command Module's Guidance Computer. These files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology", which in turn was originally created by Gary Neff, though his high-quality scans were unfortunately reduced in legibility when presented online. The markings on the front of the printout imply that it was the original AGC developer Norm Brodeur's copy. A scan by Ron Burkey has superceded it, made from a more-legible copy from the collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	ASSEMBLE REVISION 249 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS BY NASA 2021111-041
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

013100,000051:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
013101,000052:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
013102,000053:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
013103,000054:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
013104,000055: 
013105,000056:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION -
013106,000057: 
013107,000058:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
013108,000059:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
013109,000060:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
013110,000061:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
013111,000062: 
013112,000063:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
013113,000064:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
013114,000065:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
013115,000066:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
013116,000067:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
013117,000068: 
013118,000069:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
013119,000070:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
013120,000071:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
013121,000072:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
013122,000073: 
013123,000074:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
013124,000075:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
013125,000076: 
013126,000077:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
013127,000078: 
013128,000079:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
013129,000080:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
013130,000081:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
013131,000082:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
013132,000083:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
013133,000084:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013134,000085: 
013135,000086:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
013136,000087:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
013137,000088:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
013138,000089:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
013139,000090: 
013140,000091:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
013141,000092:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
013142,000093:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
013143,000094:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
013144,000095:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013145,000096: 
013146,000097:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
013147,000098: 
013148,000099:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
013149,000100:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 303 

013151,000102:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
013152,000103:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
013153,000104:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
013154,000105:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
013155,000106:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
013156,000107:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
013157,000108:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
013158,000109:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
013159,000110:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
013160,000111:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
013161,000112:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
013162,000113: 
013163,000114:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
013164,000115:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
013165,000116:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013166,000117: 
013167,000118:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
013168,000119: 
013169,000120:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013170,000121:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013171,000122:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013172,000123: 
013173,000124:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013174,000125:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013175,000126:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013176,000127:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013177,000128:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013178,000129:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013179,000130:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013180,000131: 
013181,000132:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013182,000133:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013183,000134: 
013184,000135:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
013185,000136: 
013186,000137:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013187,000138:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013188,000139:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013189,000140:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013190,000141: 
013191,000142:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
013192,000143: 
013193,000144:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013194,000145:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013195,000146:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013196,000147:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013197,000148:

Page 304 

013199,000150:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013200,000151:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013201,000152: 
013202,000153:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
013203,000154: 
013204,000155:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013205,000156:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
013206,000157: 
013207,000158:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013208,000159:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
013209,000160:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
013210,000161:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
013211,000162: 
013212,000163:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013213,000164:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013214,000165: 
013215,000166:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013216,000167:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013217,000168:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013218,000169:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013219,000170: 
013220,000171:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013221,000172:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013222,000173: 
013223,000174:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013224,000175:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
013225,000176: 
013226,000177:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013227,000178: 
013228,000179:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013229,000180:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013230,000181:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013231,000182:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013232,000183: 
013233,000184:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013234,000185:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013235,000186: 
013236,000187:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013237,000188:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
013238,000189: 
013239,000190:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013240,000191:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013241,000192:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.

Note that this doc by Green and Filene is available online — RSB 6/2004.

013246,000197: 
013247,000198:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT

013249,000200:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013250,000201:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
013251,000202:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013252,000203: 
013253,000204:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013254,000205: 
013255,000206:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013256,000207: 
013257,000208:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013258,000209:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013259,000210:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
013260,000211:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013261,000212:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013262,000213:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013263,000214:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013264,000215:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013265,000216:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013266,000217:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013267,000218:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013268,000219:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013269,000220:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013270,000221:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013271,000222:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
013272,000223:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013273,000224:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013274,000225:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013275,000226:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013276,000227:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013277,000228:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013278,000229:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013279,000230:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
013280,000231:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013281,000232:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13, C RELAYS
013282,000233:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013283,000234:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013284,000235:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013285,000236:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013286,000237:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013287,000238:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013288,000239:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013289,000240:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013290,000241:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013291,000242:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013292,000243: 
013293,000244:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013294,000245: 
013295,000246:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

013299,000250:                                                                                                  # BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
013300,000251:                                                                                                  # WRDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK

013302,000253:                                                                                                  # DECRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
013303,000254:                                                                                                  # 21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
013304,000255:                                                                                                  # UPDATRET       =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
013305,000256:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
013306,000257:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013307,000258:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013308,000259:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
013309,000260:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH

013315,000266:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
013316,000267:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = LOTEMIN-1.

013318,000269:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)

013320,000271:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = HITEMIN+1.
013321,000272:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013322,000273:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         RETURN FOR +,- ON
013323,000274:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.

013337,000288:                                                                                                  # TEM4           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013338,000289:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
013339,000290:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
013340,000291:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
013341,000292:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
013342,000293:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
013343,000294:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
013344,000295:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
013345,000296:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
013346,000297:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
013347,000298:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
013348,000299:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013349,000300:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
013350,000301:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013351,000302:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
013352,000303:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
013353,000304:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
013354,000305:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
013355,000306: 
013356,000307:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013357,000308: 
013358,000309:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013359,000310: 
013360,000311:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013361,000312:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
013362,000313:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
013363,000314:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013364,000315:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013365,000316: 
013366,000317:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013367,000318: 
013368,000319:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013369,000320: 
013370,000321:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013371,000322:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013372,000323:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013373,000324: 
013374,000325:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013375,000326: 
013376,000327:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013377,000328: 
013378,000329:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013379,000330:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013380,000331:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013381,000332: 
013382,000333:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013383,000334:

Page 308 

013385,000336:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013386,000337:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013387,000338:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013388,000339:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013389,000340:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013390,000341:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013391,000342:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013392,000343:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013393,000344:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013394,000345:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013395,000346:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013396,000347:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013397,000348: 
013398,000349:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013399,000350:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013400,000351:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013401,000352:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013402,000353:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013403,000354:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013404,000355: 
013405,000356:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013406,000357:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013407,000358:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013408,000359:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013409,000360:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013410,000361:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013411,000362: 
013412,000363:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013413,000364: 
013414,000365:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013415,000366:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013416,000367:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013417,000368:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013418,000369:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013419,000370:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013420,000371:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013421,000372:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013422,000373:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013423,000374:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013424,000375:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013425,000376: 
013426,000377:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013427,000378: 
013428,000379:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013429,000380:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013430,000381:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
013431,000382:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
013432,000383:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
013433,000384:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 309 

013435,000386:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013436,000387:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013437,000388:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013438,000389:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013439,000390:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013440,000391:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013441,000392:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013442,000393:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013443,000394: 
013444,000395:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013445,000396: 
013446,000397:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013447,000398:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013448,000399:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013449,000400:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013450,000401:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013451,000402:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013452,000403:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013453,000404:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013454,000405:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013455,000406:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013456,000407:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013457,000408: 
013458,000409:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013459,000410: 
013460,000411:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013461,000412:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013462,000413:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013463,000414:

013862,000813:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
013863,000814:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
013864,000815:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
013865,000816: 
013866,000817:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
013867,000818:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
013868,000819:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

014151,001102:

Page 325 

014153,001104:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
014154,001105: 
014155,001106:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
014156,001107:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
014157,001108:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
014158,001109:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
014159,001110:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
014160,001111: 
014161,001112:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
014162,001113:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
014163,001114: 
014164,001115:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
014165,001116: 
014166,001117:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014167,001118:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014168,001119:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014169,001120: 
014170,001121:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
014171,001122:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014172,001123:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014173,001124:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
014174,001125:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014175,001126:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
014176,001127: 
014177,001128:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014178,001129:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014179,001130:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014180,001131: 
014181,001132:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014182,001133:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014183,001134: 
014184,001135:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
014185,001136:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
014186,001137: 
014187,001138:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014188,001139: 
014189,001140:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
014190,001141:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014191,001142:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014192,001143:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
014193,001144:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014194,001145: 
014195,001146:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014196,001147:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014197,001148:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014198,001149: 
014199,001150:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014200,001151:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014201,001152: 
014202,001153:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014203,001154:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
014204,001155:

Page 326 

014206,001157:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
014207,001158: 
014208,001159: 41,2352           44711        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
014209,001160: 41,2353           02423                           TC       COMPTEST                              
014210,001161: 41,2354           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014211,001162: 41,2355           40002                           CS       2                                     
014212,001163: 41,2356           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
014213,001164: 41,2357           44712        DSPAB              CS       ONE                                   
014214,001165: 41,2360           02423                           TC       COMPTEST                              
014215,001166: 41,2361           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014216,001167: 41,2362           40001                           CS       1                                     
014217,001168: 41,2363           56131                           XCH      BUF        +1                         
014218,001169: 41,2364           02442        DSPA               TC       DECTEST                               
014219,001170: 41,2365           02465                           TC       TSTFORDP                              
014220,001171: 41,2366           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
014221,001172: 41,2367           40000                           CS       0

014507,001458:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE DISPLAYS TWO CONTIGUOUS SP POSITIVE INTEGERS
014508,001459:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
014509,001460:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED).  THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN
014510,001461:                                                                                                  #  RXD1-RXD2.
014511,001462: 
014512,001463: 40,2636           02437        2INTOUT            TC       5BLANK                                #  TO BLANK RXD3

014516,001467: 40,2642           46214                           CS       THREE

014519,001470: 40,2645           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT

014521,001472: 40,2647           30155                           CA       MPAC       +1                         
014522,001473: 40,2650           03211                           TC       DSPDECVN                              #  DISPLAY 2ND INTEGER (LIKE VERB AND NOUN)

014525,001476: 
014526,001477:                                                                                                  #  READLO PICKS UP FRESHDATA FOR BOTH HI AND LO AND LEAVES IT IN 
014527,001478:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, MPAC+1.  THIS IS NEEDED FOR TIME DISPLAY.  IT ZEROES MPAC+2, BUT

014717,001668:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
014718,001669:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
014719,001670:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
014720,001671:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

Page 349 

015315,002266:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015316,002267:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015317,002268:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015318,002269:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015319,002270:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015320,002271: 
015321,002272:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015322,002273:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015323,002274:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
015324,002275:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
015325,002276:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015326,002277:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015327,002278:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015328,002279: 
015329,002280:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015330,002281:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015331,002282:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015332,002283: 
015333,002284:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015334,002285:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015335,002286: 
015336,002287:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015337,002288:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015338,002289: 
015339,002290:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

015468,002419: 
015469,002420:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015470,002421:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
015471,002422:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
015472,002423:                                                                                                  #  
015473,002424:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015474,002425: 
015475,002426:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015476,002427:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015477,002428:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015478,002429: 
015479,002430:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015480,002431:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
015481,002432:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
015482,002433: 
015483,002434: 41,3343           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
015484,002435: 41,3344           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015485,002436: 41,3345           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015486,002437: 41,3346           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015487,002438: 41,3347           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015488,002439: 41,3350           04610                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
